Bumville!!! DO NOT COME HERE!

Before I begin my review. I usually rate places and I consider the effort the staff is providing and I think the lowest star Ive rated was 3. This place sucks!!!! I walk in and immediately had doubts as I was escorted to my seat. The place has no lively decor and the smell was like walking on an alley in the middle of Los Angeles. The food was cold and tasteless. The fried shrimp was clearly microwaved. I tried the noodles and fried rice which were cold. I tried the sushi and just took 1 bite and spat out. Did not finish the other 3 rolls I dared to get. Overall, this place needs a lot of work new owners. I would never come back here again. By the way, lots of bums come here to get a full cheap buffett under 10 bucks. They bring their odor with them.</review>
